# agent-broker >> customer-not-included (OpenBookingApprovalFlow >> Multiple)

**Booking Flow:** OpenBookingApprovalFlow

**Opportunity Type:** Multiple

**Feature:** Core / AgentBroker mode (Implemented) 

**Test:**  Customer not included in Order in AgentBroker mode

If customer is not included in Order in AgentBroker mode for C2 or B request, request should fail, returning 400 status code and IncompleteCustomerDetailsError.

### Running only this test

```bash
npm start -- --runInBand test/features/core/agent-broker/implemented/customer-not-included-test.js
```

---

âš ï¸ 74 passed with 0 failures, 937 warnings and 252 suggestions
